    1 |#
    2 |# Network services, Internet style
    3 |#
    4 |# Note that it is presently the policy of IANA to assign a single well-known
    5 |# port number for both TCP and UDP; hence, most entries here have two entries
    6 |# even if the protocol doesn't support UDP operations.
    7 |#
    8 |# This list could be found on:
    9 |#            http://www.iana.org/assignments/service-names-port-numbers/service-names-port-numbers.xml
   10 |#
   11 |# See also: services(5)
   12 |#
   13 |#
   14 |# SERVICE NAME AND TRANSPORT PROTOCOL PORT NUMBER REGISTRY
   15 |#
   16 |# (last updated on 2019-04-15)
   17 |#
   18 |# 
   19 |# Service names and port numbers are used to distinguish between different
   20 |# services that run over transport protocols such as TCP, UDP, DCCP, and
   21 |# SCTP.
   22 |# 
   23 |# Service names are assigned on a first-come, first-served process, as
   24 |# documented in [RFC6335].
   25 |# 
   26 |# Port numbers are assigned in various ways, based on three ranges: System
   27 |# Ports (0-1023), User Ports (1024-49151), and the Dynamic and/or Private
   28 |# Ports (49152-65535); the difference uses of these ranges is described in
   29 |# [RFC6335]. According to Section 8.1.2 of [RFC6335], System Ports are 
   30 |# assigned by the "IETF Review" or "IESG Approval" procedures described in 
   31 |# [RFC8126]. User Ports are assigned by IANA using the "IETF Review" process, 
   32 |# the "IESG Approval" process, or the "Expert Review" process, as per 
   33 |# [RFC6335]. Dynamic Ports are not assigned.
   34 |# 
   35 |# The registration procedures for service names and port numbers are
   36 |# described in [RFC6335].
   37 |# 
   38 |# Assigned ports both System and User ports SHOULD NOT be used without
   39 |# or prior to IANA registration.
   40 |# 
   41 |# ************************************************************************
   42 |# * PLEASE NOTE THE FOLLOWING:                                           *
   43 |# *                                                                      *
   44 |# * ASSIGNMENT OF A PORT NUMBER DOES NOT IN ANY WAY IMPLY AN             *
   45 |# * ENDORSEMENT OF AN APPLICATION OR PRODUCT, AND THE FACT THAT NETWORK  *
   46 |# * TRAFFIC IS FLOWING TO OR FROM A REGISTERED PORT DOES NOT MEAN THAT   *
   47 |# * IT IS "GOOD" TRAFFIC, NOR THAT IT NECESSARILY CORRESPONDS TO THE     *
   48 |# * ASSIGNED SERVICE. FIREWALL AND SYSTEM ADMINISTRATORS SHOULD          *
   49 |# * CHOOSE HOW TO CONFIGURE THEIR SYSTEMS BASED ON THEIR KNOWLEDGE OF    *
   50 |# * THE TRAFFIC IN QUESTION, NOT WHETHER THERE IS A PORT NUMBER          *
   51 |# * REGISTERED OR NOT.                                                   *
   52 |# ************************************************************************
   53 |#
